civilism_on_the_rise = {
	prepare_for_civilism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		available = {
			civilism > 0.1
			num_of_controlled_states > 1
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = preparation_for_civilism_civil_war }
			has_idea_with_trait = civilism_enlightener
			NOT = { has_government = civilism }
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = preparation_for_civilism_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	
	expand_civil_civilism_support = {

		icon = generic_civil_support

		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = preparation_for_civilism_civil_war
				has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_civilism
			}
			has_idea_with_trait = civilism_enlightener
			NOT = { has_government = civilism }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
		}
		
		fire_only_once = no
		
		cost = 25

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			civilism_drift = 0.05
			stability_weekly = -0.003
 			political_power_gain = -0.2
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	army_support_for_civilism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_civilism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = civilism_enlightener
			NOT = { has_government = civilism }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
		}
	
		fire_only_once = no
	
		cost = 50

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			command_power_gain = -0.2
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			set_country_flag = military_support_for_civilism_civil_war
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	ensure_general_loyalty_for_civilism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		available = {
			has_country_flag = military_support_for_civilism_civil_war
			command_power > 2
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_civilism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = civilism_enlightener
			NOT = { has_government = civilism }
			any_army_leader = {
				is_field_marshal = no
				NOT = { has_trait = hidden_sympathies }
			}
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = { id = decisions.1 }
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	ensure_marshal_loyalty_for_civilism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		available = {
			has_country_flag = military_support_for_civilism_civil_war
			command_power > 2
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_civilism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = civilism_enlightener
			NOT = { has_government = civilism }
			any_army_leader = {
				NOT = { has_trait = hidden_sympathies }
			}
			any_army_leader = {
				is_field_marshal = yes
				NOT = { has_unit_leader_flag = hidden_sympathies_marshal }
			}
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = { id = decisions.2 }
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	siphon_equipment_stockpiles_for_civilism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		available = {
			has_country_flag = military_support_for_civilism_civil_war
			has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 1000 }
			command_power > 2
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_civilism_civil_war
			has_country_flag = military_support_for_civilism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = civilism_enlightener
			NOT = { has_government = civilism }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = no
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_command_power = -2
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = -1000
			}
			set_country_flag = siphoned_equipment_stockpiles_for_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	formulate_surprise_attack_plan_for_civilism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		available = {
			has_country_flag = military_support_for_civilism_civil_war
			command_power > 2
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_civilism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = civilism_enlightener
			NOT = { has_government = civilism }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_command_power = -2
			custom_effect_tooltip = formulate_surprise_attack_plan_for_civil_war_tt
			set_country_flag = formulated_surprise_attack_plan_for_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	
	ignite_the_civilism_civil_war_single_state = {
		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war
		name = ignite_the_civilism_civil_war
		
		available = {
			has_stability < 0.5
			civilism > 0.50
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_civilism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = civilism_enlightener
			NOT = { has_government = civilism }
			check_variable = { num_owned_states = 1 }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			set_politics = { ruling_party = civilism elections_allowed = yes }
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_civilism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_civilism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_civilism_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	
	ignite_the_civilism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			has_stability < 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_civilism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = civilism_enlightener
			NOT = { has_government = civilism }
			check_variable = { num_owned_states > 1 }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@fascism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@communism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@democratic
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = conservative_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@conservative_democracy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = constitutional_monarchy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@constitutional_monarchy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = direct_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@direct_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = futurism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@futurism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = intellectualism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@intellectualism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = mythologicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@mythologicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = rightneutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@rightneutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = anarchism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@anarchism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = stupidism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@stupidism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = technicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@technicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = transformationism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@transformationism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = ruinism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@ruinism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = longitudinalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@longitudinalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = horizontalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@horizontalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = non_resistance
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@non_resistance
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = hinnulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@hinnulism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = kyonulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@kyonulism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = civilism
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_civilism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_civilism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_civilism_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	rebuild_the_nation_civilism = {

		icon = generic_construction

		visible = {
			has_government = civilism
			has_country_flag = won_ideology_civil_war
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 25

		days_remove = 365

		modifier = {
			political_power_gain = -1
			industry_repair_factor = 0.20
			production_speed_industrial_complex_factor = 0.1
			production_speed_infrastructure_factor = 0.1
			industrial_capacity_factory = 0.1
			industrial_capacity_dockyard = 0.1
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}
	}

	open_up_political_discourse_civilism = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		available = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = every_ideology_under_90
			    fascism < 0.9
			    democratic < 0.9
			    communism < 0.9
			    neutrality < 0.9
                civilism < 0.9
                conservative_democracy < 0.9
                constitutional_monarchy < 0.9
                direct_democracy < 0.9
                futurism < 0.9
                intellectualism < 0.9
                mythologicalism < 0.9
                rightneutrality < 0.9
                anarchism < 0.9
                stupidism < 0.9
                technicalism < 0.9
                neutrality_democracy < 0.9
                transformationism < 0.9
                ruinism < 0.9
                longitudinalism < 0.9
                horizontalism < 0.9
                non_resistance < 0.9
                hinnulism < 0.9
                kyonulism < 0.9
            }
		}

		visible = {
			has_idea_with_trait = civilism_enlightener
			NOT = { has_government = civilism }
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = civilism
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 75
		
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_civilism
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	discredit_government_civilism = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		available = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = every_ideology_under_80
			    fascism < 0.8
			    democratic < 0.8
			    communism < 0.8
			    neutrality < 0.8
                civilism < 0.8
                conservative_democracy < 0.8
                constitutional_monarchy < 0.8
                direct_democracy < 0.8
                futurism < 0.8
                intellectualism < 0.8
                mythologicalism < 0.8
                rightneutrality < 0.8
                anarchism < 0.8
                stupidism < 0.8
                technicalism < 0.8
                neutrality_democracy < 0.8
                transformationism < 0.8
                ruinism < 0.8
                longitudinalism < 0.8
                horizontalism < 0.8
                non_resistance < 0.8
                hinnulism < 0.8
                kyonulism < 0.8
            }
			has_idea_with_trait = civilism_enlightener
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_civilism
			NOT = { has_government = civilism }
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = civilism
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.010
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	hold_the_civilism_national_referendum = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		available = {
			civilism > 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_government = civilism }
			OR = {
				civilism > 0.6
				has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_civilism
			}
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = civilism
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 100
		
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = { id = change_ideology_event.1 }
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
			modifier = {
				civilism > 0.6
				factor = 10
			}
		}
	}
}
conservative_democracy_on_the_rise = {
	prepare_for_conservative_democracy_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		available = {
			conservative_democracy > 0.1
			num_of_controlled_states > 1
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = preparation_for_conservative_democracy_civil_war }
			has_idea_with_trait = conservative_democracy_activist
			NOT = { has_government = conservative_democracy }
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = preparation_for_conservative_democracy_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	
	expand_civil_conservative_democracy_support = {

		icon = generic_civil_support

		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = preparation_for_conservative_democracy_civil_war

			}

			NOT = { has_government = conservative_democracy }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
		}
		
		fire_only_once = no
		
		cost = 25

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			conservative_democracy_drift = 0.05
			stability_weekly = -0.003
 			political_power_gain = -0.2
		}

			factor = 1
		}
	}

		}

		}

		icon = generic_army_support

	ignite_the_conservative_democracy_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			has_stability < 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_conservative_democracy_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = conservative_democracy_activist
			NOT = { has_government = conservative_democracy }
			check_variable = { num_owned_states > 1 }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@fascism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@communism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@democratic
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = civilism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@civilism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = constitutional_monarchy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@constitutional_monarchy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = direct_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@direct_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = futurism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@futurism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = intellectualism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@intellectualism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = mythologicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@mythologicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = rightneutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@rightneutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = anarchism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@anarchism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = stupidism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@stupidism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = technicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@technicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = transformationism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@transformationism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = ruinism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@ruinism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = longitudinalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@longitudinalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = horizontalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@horizontalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = non_resistance
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@non_resistance
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = hinnulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@hinnulism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = kyonulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@kyonulism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = conservative_democracy
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_conservative_democracy_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_conservative_democracy_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_conservative_democracy_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

				}

				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}

					popularity = -0.1

			if = {

					has_government = neutrality
				}

				}

            if = {

					has_government = democratic
				}
				add_popularity = {

					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

			factor = 210

				conservative_democracy > 0.6
				factor = 10
			}
		}
	}

	expand_civil_constitutional_monarchy_support = {

		icon = generic_civil_support

		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = preparation_for_constitutional_monarchy_civil_war
				has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_constitutional_monarchy
			}
			has_idea_with_trait = constitutional_monarchist
			NOT = { has_government = constitutional_monarchy }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
		}
		
		fire_only_once = no
		
		cost = 25

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			constitutional_monarchy_drift = 0.05
			stability_weekly = -0.003
 			political_power_gain = -0.2
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	army_support_for_constitutional_monarchy_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_constitutional_monarchy_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = constitutional_monarchist
			NOT = { has_government = constitutional_monarchy }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
		}
	
		fire_only_once = no
	
		cost = 50

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			command_power_gain = -0.2
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			set_country_flag = military_support_for_constitutional_monarchy_civil_war
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

					value = party_popularity@technicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = transformationism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@transformationism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = ruinism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@ruinism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = longitudinalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@longitudinalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = horizontalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@horizontalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = non_resistance
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@non_resistance
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = hinnulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@hinnulism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = kyonulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@kyonulism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = constitutional_monarchy
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_constitutional_monarchy_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_constitutional_monarchy_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_constitutional_monarchy_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

			set_country_flag = military_support_for_direct_democracy_civil_war

		}

			factor = 0

                direct_democracy < 0.8
                futurism < 0.8
                intellectualism < 0.8
                mythologicalism < 0.8
                rightneutrality < 0.8
                anarchism < 0.8
                stupidism < 0.8
                technicalism < 0.8
                neutrality_democracy < 0.8
                transformationism < 0.8
                ruinism < 0.8
                longitudinalism < 0.8
                horizontalism < 0.8
                non_resistance < 0.8
                hinnulism < 0.8
                kyonulism < 0.8
            }
			has_idea_with_trait = direct_democracy_campaigner
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_direct_democracy
			NOT = { has_government = direct_democracy }
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = direct_democracy
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.010
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	hold_the_direct_democracy_national_referendum = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		available = {
			direct_democracy > 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_government = direct_democracy }
			OR = {
				direct_democracy > 0.6
				has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_direct_democracy
			}
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = direct_democracy
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 100
		
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = { id = change_ideology_event.4 }
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
			modifier = {
				direct_democracy > 0.6
				factor = 10
			}
		}
	}

	army_support_for_futurism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

			has_country_flag = preparation_for_futurism_civil_war

		cost = 50

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			command_power_gain = -0.2
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			set_country_flag = military_support_for_futurism_civil_war
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}

	ignite_the_futurism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			has_stability < 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_futurism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = futuric_thinker
			NOT = { has_government = futurism }
			check_variable = { num_owned_states > 1 }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@fascism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@communism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@democratic
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = civilism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@civilism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = conservative_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@conservative_democracy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = constitutional_monarchy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@constitutional_monarchy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = direct_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@direct_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = intellectualism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@intellectualism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = mythologicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@mythologicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = rightneutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@rightneutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = anarchism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@anarchism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = stupidism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@stupidism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = technicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@technicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = transformationism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@transformationism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = ruinism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@ruinism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = longitudinalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@longitudinalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = horizontalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@horizontalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = non_resistance
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@non_resistance
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = hinnulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@hinnulism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = kyonulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@kyonulism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = futurism
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_futurism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_futurism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_futurism_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	ignite_the_intellectualism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			has_stability < 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_intellectualism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = intelligentsia
			NOT = { has_government = intellectualism }
			check_variable = { num_owned_states > 1 }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@fascism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@communism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@democratic
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = civilism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@civilism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = conservative_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@conservative_democracy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = constitutional_monarchy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@constitutional_monarchy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = direct_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@direct_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = futurism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@futurism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = mythologicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@mythologicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = rightneutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@rightneutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = anarchism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@anarchism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = stupidism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@stupidism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = technicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@technicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = transformationism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@transformationism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = ruinism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@ruinism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = longitudinalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@longitudinalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = horizontalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@horizontalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = non_resistance
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@non_resistance
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = hinnulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@hinnulism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = kyonulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@kyonulism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = intellectualism
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_intellectualism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_intellectualism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_intellectualism_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

			industrial_capacity_factory = 0.1
			industrial_capacity_dockyard = 0.1
		}

		}

                ruinism < 0.9
                longitudinalism < 0.9
                horizontalism < 0.9
                non_resistance < 0.9
                hinnulism < 0.9
                kyonulism < 0.9
            }
		}

		visible = {
			has_idea_with_trait = intelligentsia
			NOT = { has_government = intellectualism }
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = intellectualism
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes

		available = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = every_ideology_under_80
			    fascism < 0.8
			    democratic < 0.8

                direct_democracy < 0.8
                futurism < 0.8
                intellectualism < 0.8

                rightneutrality < 0.8
                anarchism < 0.8
                stupidism < 0.8
                technicalism < 0.8
                neutrality_democracy < 0.8
                transformationism < 0.8
                ruinism < 0.8
                longitudinalism < 0.8
                horizontalism < 0.8
                non_resistance < 0.8
                hinnulism < 0.8
                kyonulism < 0.8
            }
			has_idea_with_trait = intelligentsia
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_intellectualism
			NOT = { has_government = intellectualism }
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = intellectualism
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.010
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
			modifier = {
				intellectualism > 0.6
				factor = 10
			}
		}
	}

		icon = generic_civil_support

		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = preparation_for_mythologicalism_civil_war
				has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_mythologicalism
			}
			has_idea_with_trait = devout_believer
			NOT = { has_government = mythologicalism }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
		}
		
		fire_only_once = no
		
		cost = 25

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			mythologicalism_drift = 0.05
			stability_weekly = -0.003
 			political_power_gain = -0.2
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	army_support_for_mythologicalism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_mythologicalism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = devout_believer
			NOT = { has_government = mythologicalism }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
		}
	
		fire_only_once = no
	
		cost = 50

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			command_power_gain = -0.2
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			set_country_flag = military_support_for_mythologicalism_civil_war
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

				}

				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var

			if = {
				limit = {

						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}

				ruling_party = mythologicalism
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_mythologicalism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_mythologicalism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_mythologicalism_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}

			NOT = { has_government = anarchism }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {

			}
		}

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {

 			political_power_gain = -0.2

	army_support_for_anarchism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_anarchism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = anarchist
			NOT = { has_government = anarchism }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
		}
	
		fire_only_once = no
	
		cost = 50

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			command_power_gain = -0.2
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			set_country_flag = military_support_for_anarchism_civil_war
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	ignite_the_anarchism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			has_stability < 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_anarchism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = anarchist
			NOT = { has_government = anarchism }
			check_variable = { num_owned_states > 1 }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@fascism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@communism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@democratic
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = civilism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@civilism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = conservative_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@conservative_democracy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = constitutional_monarchy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@constitutional_monarchy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = direct_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@direct_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = futurism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@futurism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = intellectualism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@intellectualism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = mythologicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@mythologicalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = rightneutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@rightneutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = stupidism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@stupidism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = technicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@technicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = transformationism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@transformationism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = ruinism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@ruinism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = longitudinalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@longitudinalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = horizontalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@horizontalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = non_resistance
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@non_resistance
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = hinnulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@hinnulism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = kyonulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@kyonulism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = anarchism
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_anarchism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_anarchism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_anarchism_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	army_support_for_stupidism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_stupidism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = stupid_trait
			NOT = { has_government = stupidism }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
		}
	
		fire_only_once = no
	
		cost = 50

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			command_power_gain = -0.2
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			set_country_flag = military_support_for_stupidism_civil_war
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	ignite_the_stupidism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			has_stability < 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_stupidism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = stupid_trait
			NOT = { has_government = stupidism }
			check_variable = { num_owned_states > 1 }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@fascism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@communism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@democratic
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = civilism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@civilism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = conservative_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@conservative_democracy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = constitutional_monarchy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@constitutional_monarchy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = direct_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@direct_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = futurism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@futurism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = intellectualism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@intellectualism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = mythologicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@mythologicalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = rightneutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@rightneutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = anarchism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@anarchism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = technicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@technicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = transformationism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@transformationism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = ruinism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@ruinism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = longitudinalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@longitudinalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = horizontalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@horizontalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = non_resistance
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@non_resistance
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = hinnulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@hinnulism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = kyonulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@kyonulism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = stupidism
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_stupidism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_stupidism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_stupidism_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

                longitudinalism < 0.9
                horizontalism < 0.9
                non_resistance < 0.9
                hinnulism < 0.9
                kyonulism < 0.9
            }
		}

		visible = {
			has_idea_with_trait = stupid_trait
			NOT = { has_government = stupidism }

		remove_trigger = {

	discredit_government_stupidism = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		available = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = every_ideology_under_80
			    fascism < 0.8
			    democratic < 0.8
			    communism < 0.8
			    neutrality < 0.8
                civilism < 0.8
                conservative_democracy < 0.8
                constitutional_monarchy < 0.8
                direct_democracy < 0.8
                futurism < 0.8
                intellectualism < 0.8
                mythologicalism < 0.8
                rightneutrality < 0.8
                anarchism < 0.8
                stupidism < 0.8
                technicalism < 0.8
                neutrality_democracy < 0.8
                transformationism < 0.8
                ruinism < 0.8
                longitudinalism < 0.8
                horizontalism < 0.8
                non_resistance < 0.8
                hinnulism < 0.8
                kyonulism < 0.8
            }
			has_idea_with_trait = stupid_trait
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_stupidism
			NOT = { has_government = stupidism }
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = stupidism
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.010
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

		cost = 100
		
		complete_effect = {

		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
			modifier = {
				stupidism > 0.6
				factor = 10
			}
		}
	}

			factor = 0

				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			set_country_flag = military_support_for_neutrality_democracy_civil_war
		}

		}

			factor = 0

				limit = {
					has_government = non_resistance
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@non_resistance
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = hinnulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@hinnulism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = kyonulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@kyonulism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = neutrality_democracy
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_neutrality_democracy_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_neutrality_democracy_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_neutrality_democracy_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

            if = {

					has_government = democratic
				}

				}

		}

		icon = generic_army_support

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_transformationism_civil_war

			NOT = { has_government = transformationism }

			command_power_gain = -0.2
		}

			if = {
				limit = {

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			set_country_flag = military_support_for_transformationism_civil_war
		}

		}

			factor = 0

					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	hold_the_transformationism_national_referendum = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		available = {
			transformationism > 0.5
		}

		visible = {

				transformationism > 0.6

				factor = 10
			}
		}

			hidden_trigger = {

			}

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {

 			political_power_gain = -0.2

	army_support_for_ruinism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_ruinism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = ruin_bringer
			NOT = { has_government = ruinism }

		fire_only_once = no
	
		cost = 50

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			command_power_gain = -0.2
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			set_country_flag = military_support_for_ruinism_civil_war
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	ignite_the_ruinism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			has_stability < 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_ruinism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = ruin_bringer
			NOT = { has_government = ruinism }
			check_variable = { num_owned_states > 1 }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@fascism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@communism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@democratic
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = civilism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@civilism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = conservative_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@conservative_democracy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = constitutional_monarchy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@constitutional_monarchy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = direct_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@direct_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = futurism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@futurism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = intellectualism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@intellectualism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = mythologicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@mythologicalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = rightneutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@rightneutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = anarchism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@anarchism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = stupidism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@stupidism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = technicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@technicalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = transformationism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@transformationism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = longitudinalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@longitudinalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = horizontalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@horizontalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = non_resistance
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@non_resistance
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = hinnulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@hinnulism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = kyonulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@kyonulism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = ruinism
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_ruinism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_ruinism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_ruinism_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

			has_country_flag = military_support_for_longitudinalism_civil_war
			has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 1000 }
			command_power > 2
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_longitudinalism_civil_war
			has_country_flag = military_support_for_longitudinalism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = longitudinalist
			NOT = { has_government = longitudinalism }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = no
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_command_power = -2
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = -1000
			}
			set_country_flag = siphoned_equipment_stockpiles_for_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	formulate_surprise_attack_plan_for_longitudinalism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		available = {
			has_country_flag = military_support_for_longitudinalism_civil_war
			command_power > 2
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_longitudinalism_civil_war

	ignite_the_longitudinalism_civil_war_single_state = {
		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war
		name = ignite_the_longitudinalism_civil_war
		
		available = {
			has_stability < 0.5
			longitudinalism > 0.50
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_longitudinalism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = longitudinalist
			NOT = { has_government = longitudinalism }
			check_variable = { num_owned_states = 1 }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			set_politics = { ruling_party = longitudinalism elections_allowed = yes }
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_longitudinalism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_longitudinalism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_longitudinalism_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}

	ignite_the_longitudinalism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			has_stability < 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_longitudinalism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = longitudinalist
			NOT = { has_government = longitudinalism }
			check_variable = { num_owned_states > 1 }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@fascism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@communism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@democratic
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = civilism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@civilism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = conservative_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@conservative_democracy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = constitutional_monarchy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@constitutional_monarchy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = direct_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@direct_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = futurism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@futurism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = intellectualism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@intellectualism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = mythologicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@mythologicalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = rightneutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@rightneutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = anarchism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@anarchism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = stupidism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@stupidism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = technicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@technicalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = transformationism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@transformationism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = ruinism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@ruinism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = horizontalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@horizontalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = non_resistance
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@non_resistance
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = hinnulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@hinnulism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = kyonulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@kyonulism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = longitudinalism
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_longitudinalism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_longitudinalism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_longitudinalism_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	rebuild_the_nation_longitudinalism = {

		icon = generic_construction

		visible = {
			has_government = longitudinalism
			has_country_flag = won_ideology_civil_war
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 25

		days_remove = 365

		modifier = {
			political_power_gain = -1
			industry_repair_factor = 0.20
			production_speed_industrial_complex_factor = 0.1
			production_speed_infrastructure_factor = 0.1
			industrial_capacity_factory = 0.1
			industrial_capacity_dockyard = 0.1
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}
	}

	open_up_political_discourse_longitudinalism = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		available = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = every_ideology_under_90
			    fascism < 0.9
			    democratic < 0.9
			    communism < 0.9
			    neutrality < 0.9
                civilism < 0.9
                conservative_democracy < 0.9
                constitutional_monarchy < 0.9
                direct_democracy < 0.9
                futurism < 0.9
                intellectualism < 0.9
                mythologicalism < 0.9
                rightneutrality < 0.9
                anarchism < 0.9
                stupidism < 0.9
                technicalism < 0.9
                neutrality_democracy < 0.9
                transformationism < 0.9
                ruinism < 0.9
                longitudinalism < 0.9
                horizontalism < 0.9
                non_resistance < 0.9
                hinnulism < 0.9
                kyonulism < 0.9
            }
		}

		visible = {
			has_idea_with_trait = longitudinalist
			NOT = { has_government = longitudinalism }
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = longitudinalism
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 75
		
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_longitudinalism
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	discredit_government_longitudinalism = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		available = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = every_ideology_under_80
			    fascism < 0.8
			    democratic < 0.8
			    communism < 0.8
			    neutrality < 0.8
                civilism < 0.8
                conservative_democracy < 0.8
                constitutional_monarchy < 0.8
                direct_democracy < 0.8
                futurism < 0.8
                intellectualism < 0.8
                mythologicalism < 0.8
                rightneutrality < 0.8
                anarchism < 0.8
                stupidism < 0.8
                technicalism < 0.8
                neutrality_democracy < 0.8
                transformationism < 0.8
                ruinism < 0.8
                longitudinalism < 0.8
                horizontalism < 0.8
                non_resistance < 0.8
                hinnulism < 0.8
                kyonulism < 0.8
            }
			has_idea_with_trait = longitudinalist
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_longitudinalism
			NOT = { has_government = longitudinalism }
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = longitudinalism
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.010
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	hold_the_longitudinalism_national_referendum = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		available = {
			longitudinalism > 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_government = longitudinalism }
			OR = {
				longitudinalism > 0.6
				has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_longitudinalism
			}
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = longitudinalism
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 100
		
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = { id = change_ideology_event.15 }
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
			modifier = {
				longitudinalism > 0.6
				factor = 10
			}
		}
	}
}
horizontalism_on_the_rise = {
	prepare_for_horizontalism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		available = {
			horizontalism > 0.1
			num_of_controlled_states > 1
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = preparation_for_horizontalism_civil_war }
			has_idea_with_trait = horizontalist
			NOT = { has_government = horizontalism }
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = preparation_for_horizontalism_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	
	expand_civil_horizontalism_support = {

		icon = generic_civil_support

		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = preparation_for_horizontalism_civil_war
				has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_horizontalism
			}
			has_idea_with_trait = horizontalist
			NOT = { has_government = horizontalism }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
		}
		
		fire_only_once = no
		
		cost = 25

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			horizontalism_drift = 0.05
			stability_weekly = -0.003
 			political_power_gain = -0.2
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	army_support_for_horizontalism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_horizontalism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = horizontalist
			NOT = { has_government = horizontalism }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
		}
	
		fire_only_once = no
	
		cost = 50

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			command_power_gain = -0.2
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			set_country_flag = military_support_for_horizontalism_civil_war
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	ensure_general_loyalty_for_horizontalism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		available = {
			has_country_flag = military_support_for_horizontalism_civil_war
			command_power > 2
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_horizontalism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = horizontalist
			NOT = { has_government = horizontalism }
			any_army_leader = {
				is_field_marshal = no
				NOT = { has_trait = hidden_sympathies }
			}
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = { id = decisions.1 }
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
