					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@anarchism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = stupidism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@stupidism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = technicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@technicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = transformationism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@transformationism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = ruinism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@ruinism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = longitudinalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@longitudinalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = non_resistance
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@non_resistance
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = hinnulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@hinnulism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = kyonulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@kyonulism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = horizontalism
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_horizontalism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_horizontalism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_horizontalism_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

			if = {

            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
		}

			factor = 1
		}
	}

			set_country_flag = military_support_for_non_resistance_civil_war

		}

                neutrality_democracy < 0.8
                transformationism < 0.8
                ruinism < 0.8
                longitudinalism < 0.8
                horizontalism < 0.8
                non_resistance < 0.8
                hinnulism < 0.8
                kyonulism < 0.8
            }
			has_idea_with_trait = dependentist
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_non_resistance
			NOT = { has_government = non_resistance }
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = non_resistance
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.010
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	hold_the_non_resistance_national_referendum = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		available = {
			non_resistance > 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_government = non_resistance }
			OR = {
				non_resistance > 0.6
				has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_non_resistance
			}
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = non_resistance
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 100
		
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = { id = change_ideology_event.17 }
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
			modifier = {
				non_resistance > 0.6
				factor = 10
			}
		}
	}

	army_support_for_hinnulism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

			has_country_flag = preparation_for_hinnulism_civil_war

		cost = 50

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			command_power_gain = -0.2
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			set_country_flag = military_support_for_hinnulism_civil_war
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}

	ignite_the_hinnulism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			has_stability < 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_hinnulism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = hinnulist
			NOT = { has_government = hinnulism }
			check_variable = { num_owned_states > 1 }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@fascism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@communism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@democratic
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = civilism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@civilism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = conservative_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@conservative_democracy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = constitutional_monarchy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@constitutional_monarchy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = direct_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@direct_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = futurism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@futurism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = intellectualism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@intellectualism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = mythologicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@mythologicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = rightneutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@rightneutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = anarchism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@anarchism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = stupidism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@stupidism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = technicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@technicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = transformationism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@transformationism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = ruinism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@ruinism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = longitudinalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@longitudinalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = horizontalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@horizontalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = non_resistance
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@non_resistance
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = kyonulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@kyonulism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = hinnulism
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_hinnulism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_hinnulism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_hinnulism_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	ignite_the_kyonulism_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			has_stability < 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_kyonulism_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = kyonulist
			NOT = { has_government = kyonulism }
			check_variable = { num_owned_states > 1 }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@fascism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@communism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@democratic
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = civilism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@civilism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = conservative_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@conservative_democracy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = constitutional_monarchy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@constitutional_monarchy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = direct_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@direct_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = futurism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@futurism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = intellectualism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@intellectualism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = mythologicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@mythologicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = rightneutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@rightneutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = anarchism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@anarchism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = stupidism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@stupidism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = technicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@technicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = transformationism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@transformationism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = ruinism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@ruinism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = longitudinalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@longitudinalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = horizontalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@horizontalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = non_resistance
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@non_resistance
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = hinnulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@hinnulism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = kyonulism
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_kyonulism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_kyonulism_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_kyonulism_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

		}

		}

                ruinism < 0.9
                longitudinalism < 0.9
                horizontalism < 0.9
                non_resistance < 0.9
                hinnulism < 0.9
                kyonulism < 0.9
            }
		}

		visible = {
			has_idea_with_trait = kyonulist
			NOT = { has_government = kyonulism }
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		available = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = every_ideology_under_80
			    fascism < 0.8

			    communism < 0.8

                direct_democracy < 0.8
                futurism < 0.8

                rightneutrality < 0.8
                anarchism < 0.8
                stupidism < 0.8
                technicalism < 0.8
                neutrality_democracy < 0.8
                transformationism < 0.8
                ruinism < 0.8
                longitudinalism < 0.8
                horizontalism < 0.8
                non_resistance < 0.8
                hinnulism < 0.8
                kyonulism < 0.8
            }
			has_idea_with_trait = kyonulist
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_kyonulism
			NOT = { has_government = kyonulism }
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = kyonulism
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 50
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.010
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

			OR = {
				has_country_flag = preparation_for_neutrality_civil_war
				has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_neutrality

			has_idea_with_trait = trait_centrist
			NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
		}
		
		fire_only_once = no
		
		cost = 25

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			neutrality_drift = 0.05

 			political_power_gain = -0.2

			factor = 1

	army_support_for_neutrality_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_neutrality_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = trait_centrist
			NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
		}
	
		fire_only_once = no
	
		cost = 50

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			command_power_gain = -0.2
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 } 
			}
			set_country_flag = military_support_for_neutrality_civil_war
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

					has_government = conservative_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@conservative_democracy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = constitutional_monarchy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@constitutional_monarchy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = direct_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@direct_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = futurism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@futurism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = intellectualism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@intellectualism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = mythologicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@mythologicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = rightneutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@rightneutrality
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = anarchism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@anarchism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = stupidism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@stupidism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = technicalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@technicalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality_democracy
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality_democracy
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = transformationism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@transformationism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = ruinism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@ruinism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = longitudinalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@longitudinalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = horizontalism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@horizontalism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = non_resistance
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@non_resistance
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = hinnulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@hinnulism
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = kyonulism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@kyonulism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_neutrality_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_neutrality_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_neutrality_civil_war
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	rebuild_the_nation_neutrality = {

		icon = generic_construction

		visible = {
			has_government = neutrality
			has_country_flag = won_ideology_civil_war
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
	
		cost = 25

		days_remove = 365

		modifier = {
			political_power_gain = -1
			industry_repair_factor = 0.20
			production_speed_industrial_complex_factor = 0.1
			production_speed_infrastructure_factor = 0.1
			industrial_capacity_factory = 0.1
			industrial_capacity_dockyard = 0.1
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}
	}

	open_up_political_discourse_neutrality = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		available = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = every_ideology_under_90
			    fascism < 0.9
			    democratic < 0.9
			    communism < 0.9
			    neutrality < 0.9
                civilism < 0.9
                conservative_democracy < 0.9
                constitutional_monarchy < 0.9
                direct_democracy < 0.9
                futurism < 0.9
                intellectualism < 0.9
                mythologicalism < 0.9
                rightneutrality < 0.9
                anarchism < 0.9
                stupidism < 0.9
                technicalism < 0.9
                neutrality_democracy < 0.9
                transformationism < 0.9
                ruinism < 0.9
                longitudinalism < 0.9
                horizontalism < 0.9
                non_resistance < 0.9
                hinnulism < 0.9
                kyonulism < 0.9
            }
		}

		visible = {
			has_idea_with_trait = trait_centrist
			NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = neutrality
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 75
		
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_neutrality
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	discredit_government_neutrality = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		available = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {

                civilism < 0.8
                conservative_democracy < 0.8
                constitutional_monarchy < 0.8
                direct_democracy < 0.8
                futurism < 0.8
                intellectualism < 0.8
                mythologicalism < 0.8
                rightneutrality < 0.8
                anarchism < 0.8
                stupidism < 0.8
                technicalism < 0.8
                neutrality_democracy < 0.8
                transformationism < 0.8
                ruinism < 0.8
                longitudinalism < 0.8
                horizontalism < 0.8
                non_resistance < 0.8
                hinnulism < 0.8
                kyonulism < 0.8
            }
			has_idea_with_trait = trait_centrist
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_neutrality
			NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = neutrality
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 50

					has_government = fascism
				}

					ideology = fascism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				add_popularity = {

					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
            if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
		}

		}
	}
	
	hold_the_neutrality_national_referendum = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		available = {
			neutrality > 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
			OR = {
				neutrality > 0.6
				has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_neutrality
			}
		}
		
		remove_trigger = {
			has_government = neutrality
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 100
		
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = { id = change_ideology_event.20 }
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
			modifier = {
				neutrality > 0.6
				factor = 10
			}
		}
	}
